14/09/22, 16:08 - Himral: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
#define n 20
class queue
{
    int *arr;
    int front;
    int back;
public:
    queue()
    {
        arr = new int[n];
        front = -1;
        back = -1;
    }
    void push(int x)
    {
        if (back == n - 1)
        {
            cout << "Queue Overflow" << endl;
            return;
        }
        back++;
        arr[back] = x;

        if (front == -1)
        {
            front++;
        }
    }
    void pop()
    {
        if (front == -1 || front > back)
        {
            cout << "No elements in queue\n";
            return;
        }
        front++;
    }
    int peek()
    {
        if (front == -1 || front > back)
        {
            cout << "No elemets in queue" << endl;
            return -1;
        }
        return arr[front];
    }
    bool empty()
    {
        if (front == -1 || front > back)
        {

            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}; 
int main()
{
    queue q;
    q.push(1);
    q.push(2);
    q.push(3);
    cout << q.peek() << endl;
}

    <script>  
            function validation()  
            {  
                var id=document.f1.user.value;  
                var ps=document.f1.pass.value;  
                if(id.length=="" && ps.length=="") {  
                    alert("User Name and Password fields are empty");  
                    return false;  
                }  
                else  
                {  
                    if(id.length=="") {  
                        alert("User Name is empty");  
                        return false;  
                    }   
                    if (ps.length=="") {  
                    alert("Password field is empty");  
                    return false;  
                    }  
                }                             
            }  
        </script>  
</body>

Here are few ideas for the project that can be built upon:
26/04/23, 18:22 - Vidhi 💕: Route Planning: Implement a program that plans the most efficient route for an airplane to travel between two cities, taking into account factors such as fuel consumption, flight time, and weather conditions.

Here's an outline of how you can implement a route planning program that uses dynamic programming:

1. Define a data structure to represent the graph of airports and flights. You can use an adjacency matrix or an adjacency list to represent the graph.

2. Define a data structure to represent the state of the airplane, including its current location, fuel level, and other relevant information.

3. Define a function to calculate the optimal flight path using dynamic programming. This function should take as input the start and end cities, as well as the state of the airplane, and should return the optimal flight path.

4. Define a function to calculate the fuel consumption for a given flight. This function should take as input the distance, the airplane type, and other relevant information, and should return the fuel consumption for the flight.

5. Use Dijkstra's algorithm or a similar algorithm to calculate the shortest path between the start and end cities, taking into account the fuel consumption for each flight.

6. Use dynamic programming to optimise the flight path and minimise travel time, taking into account weather conditions, air traffic, and other relevant factors.
26/04/23, 18:22 - Vidhi 💕: int dp[N][M]; // dp[i][j] represents the minimum time to reach city i with j fuel remaining
for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for (int j = 0; j < M; j++) {
        dp[i][j] = INF;
    }
}
dp[start_city][initial_fuel] = 0;

for (int j = initial_fuel; j >= 0; j--) {
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        for (auto& flight : flights[i]) {
            int next_city = flight.to;
            int fuel_cost = flight.fuel_cost;
            int flight_time = flight.time;

            if (j >= fuel_cost && dp[i][j] + flight_time < dp[next_city][j - fuel_cost]) {
                dp[next_city][j - fuel_cost] = dp[i][j] + flight_time;
            }
        }
    }
}

This code calculates the minimum time to reach each city from the starting city, taking into account the fuel consumption for each flight. The variable flights[i] represents the list of flights that depart from city i.

#include <iostream>

#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;

const int MAX_CITIES = 100;
const int MAX_FUEL = 100;
const int MAX_WIND_SPEED = 10;
const int INF = 1000000000;

struct Flight {
    int to;
    int distance;
};

vector<Flight> flights[MAX_CITIES];
int dp[MAX_CITIES][MAX_FUEL][MAX_WIND_SPEED];

int calculate_fuel_cost(int distance, int airplane_type, int wind_speed, int wind_direction) {
    // Calculate the fuel cost for a given flight, taking into account the wind speed and direction, the airplane type, and other relevant factors.

    // ...

    // Return the flight time as an integer value.

vector<int> calculate_optimal_flight_path(int start_city, int end_city, int initial_fuel, int initial_wind_speed) {
    int N = flights.size();
    int M = initial_fuel + 1;
    int K = MAX_WIND_SPEED + 1;

    // Initialize the dynamic programming table with large values
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < M; j++) {
            for (int k = 0; k < K; k++) {
                dp[i][j][k] = INF;
            }
        }
    }

    // Initialize the starting city with initial fuel and wind speed
    dp[start_city][initial_fuel][initial_wind_speed] = 0;

    // Use dynamic programming to calculate the optimal flight path
    for (int j = initial_fuel; j >= 0; j--) {
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
            for (auto& flight : flights[i]) {
                int next_city = flight.to;
                int fuel_cost = calculate_fuel_cost(flight.distance, airplane_type, wind_speed, wind_direction);
                int flight_time = calculate_flight_time(flight.distance, airplane_type, wind_speed, wind_direction);

                for (int k = 0; k < K; k++) {
                    int next_wind_speed = calculate_next_wind_speed(wind_speed, wind_direction, time_step);
                    if (j >= fuel_cost && dp[i][j][k] + flight_time < dp[next_city][j - fuel_cost][next_wind_speed]) {
                        dp[next_city][j - fuel_cost][next_wind_speed] = dp[i][j][k] + flight_time;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

26/04/23, 18:59 - Vidhi 💕: This code below is to implement Collision Avoidance: Create a program that uses dynamic programming to determine the optimal course of action for an airplane to avoid a potential collision with another aircraft. This can be accomplished by calculating the optimal trajectory for the airplane while taking into account the location and trajectory of the other aircraft.




#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;

const int MAX_TIME = 100;
const int MAX_SPEED = 10;
const int MAX_TURN = 5;
const int INF = 1000000000;

struct Aircraft {
    int x, y, z; // current position
    int speed; // current speed
    int heading; // current heading
};

int dp[MAX_TIME][MAX_SPEED][MAX_TURN][MAX_SPEED][MAX_TURN];

int calculate_distance(const Aircraft& a1, const Aircraft& a2) {
    // Calculate the distance between two aircraft, taking into account their current positions and other relevant factors.
    // Return the distance as an integer value.
    // ...
}

int calculate_time_to_collision(const Aircraft& a1, const Aircraft& a2) {
    // Calculate the time until collision between two aircraft, taking into account their current positions, speeds, headings, and other relevant factors.
    // Return the time until collision as an integer value.
    // ...
}

int calculate_required_speed_change(int current_speed, int target_speed) {
    // Calculate the required speed change to reach a target speed, taking into account the current speed and other relevant factors.
    // Return the required speed change as an integer value.
    // ...
}

int calculate_required_turn(int current_heading, int target_heading) {
    // Calculate the required turn to reach a target heading, taking into account the current heading and other relevant factors.
    // Return the required turn as an integer value.
    // ...
}

int calculate_optimal_collision_avoidance(int t, const Aircraft& a1, const Aircraft& a2) {
    int d = calculate_distance(a1, a2);
    int T = calculate_time_to_collision(a1, a2);
    int S1 = a1.speed;
    int S2 = a2.speed;
    int H1 = a1.heading;
    int H2 = a2.heading;
    int N1 = MAX_SPEED + 1;
    int N2 = MAX_TURN + 1;

    // Initialize the dynamic programming table with large values
    for (int i = 0; i <= N1; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j <= N2; j++) {
            for (int k = 0; k <= N1; k++) {
                for (int l = 0; l <= N2; l++) {
                    dp[t][i][j][k][l] = INF;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Base case: if the two aircraft are already on a collision course, the optimal action is to immediately slow down or turn away
    if (T <= t) {
        return 0;
    }

    // Use dynamic programming to calculate the optimal collision avoidance action
    for (int i = 0; i <= N1; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j <= N2; j++) {
            for (int k = 0; k <= N1; k++) {
                for (int l = 0; l <= N2; l++) {
                    int new_speed1 = S1 + i - k;
                    int new_speed2 = S2 + k - i;
                    int new_heading1 = H1 + j - l;
                    int new_heading2 = H2 + l - j;

                    // Check that the new speeds and headings are within acceptable ranges
                    if (new_speed1 >= 0 && new_speed1 <= MAX_SPEED && new_speed2 >= 0 && new_speed2 <= MAX_SPEED &&
                        new_heading1 >= 0 && new_heading1 <= 359 && new_heading2 >= 0 && new_heading2 <= 359) {

                        int cost = calculate_cost(d, T, i, k, j, l);

                        if (t == MAX_TIME) {
                            // If we're at the end of the planning horizon, store the cost in the dynamic programming table
                            dp[t][i][j][k][l] = cost;
                        } else {
                            // Otherwise, recursively calculate the cost of future collision avoidance actions
                            for (int m = 0; m <= N1; m++) {
                                for (int n = 0; n <= N2; n++) {
                                    for (int o = 0; o <= N1; o++) {
                                        for (int p = 0; p <= N2; p++) {
                                            int new_t = t + 1;
                                            int new_d = d + calculate_new_distance(d, T, new_speed1, new_speed2);
                                            int sub_cost = dp[new_t][m][n][o][p];
                                            int total_cost = cost + sub_cost;

                                            // Update the dynamic programming table with the minimum cost
                                            dp[t][i][j][k][l] = min(dp[t][i][j][k][l], total_cost);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Return the optimal collision avoidance cost for the current time and aircraft

// Calculate the cost of taking a particular action, taking into account factors such as fuel consumption and time
int calculate_cost(int current_cost, int new_speed1, int new_speed2, int new_heading1, int new_heading2) {
    // You can define the cost function based on the specific requirements of the problem
    // For example, the cost could be a function of the time, fuel consumption, distance traveled, etc.
    // ...
    int new_cost = current_cost + 1; // A simple cost function that just increments the cost by 1
    return new_cost;
}

// Calculate the new distance between two aircraft after a particular action has been taken
int calculate_new_distance(const Aircraft& a1, const Aircraft& a2, int new_speed1, int new_speed2, int new_heading1, int new_heading2) {
    // Calculate the new positions of the aircraft based on the new speeds and headings, and then calculate the new distance
    // ...
    int new_x1 = a1.x + new_speed1 * cos(new_heading1);
    int new_y1 = a1.y + new_speed1 * sin(new_heading1);
    int new_z1 = a1.z;
    int new_x2 = a2.x + new_speed2 * cos(new_heading2);
    int new_y2 = a2.y + new_speed2 * sin(new_heading2);
    int new_z2 = a2.z;
    Aircraft new_a1 = {new_x1, new_y1, new_z1, new_speed1, new_heading1};
    Aircraft new_a2 = {new_x2, new_y2, new_z2, new_speed2, new_heading2};
    int new_distance = calculate_distance(new_a1, new_a2);
    return new_distance;
}

27/04/23, 22:17 - Vidhi 💕: Write a c++ code for a program that uses dynammic programming to calculate the optimal flight path for an airplane given a set of constraints such as wind speed, air traffic, and weather conditions. The code should be based on foloowing outline:
1. Define a data structure to represent the state of the airplane, including its current location, fuel level, and other relevant information.

2. Define a data structure to represent the weather conditions, including wind speed and direction, temperature, and humidity.

3. Define a data structure to represent the air traffic, including the positions and trajectories of other aircraft.

4. Define a function to calculate the optimal flight path using dynamic programming. This function should take as input the start and end cities, as well as the state of the airplane, the weather conditions, and the air traffic, and should return the optimal flight path.

5. Define a function to calculate the fuel consumption for a given flight, taking into account the wind speed and direction, the airplane type, and other relevant factors.

6. Use dynamic programming to optimize the flight path and minimize travel time, taking into account the weather conditions, air traffic, and other relevant factors.


// Defining data structures
struct airplaneState {
    // Current location
    int locationX;
    int locationY;
    
    // Fuel level
    int fuelLevel;
};

struct weatherConditions {
    // Wind speed
    int windSpeed;
    // Wind direction
    int windDirection;
    // Temperature
    int temperature;
    // Humidity
    int humidity;
};

struct airTraffic {
    // Positions
    int positionX;
    int positionY;
    // Trajectories
    int trajectoryX;
    int trajectoryY;
};

// Defining the function to calculate the optimal flight path
vector<int> calculateOptimalFlightPath(int startCity, int endCity, airplaneState &airplane, weatherConditions &weather, airTraffic &airTraffic) {
    // Initializing the optimal flight path vector
    vector<int> optimalFlightPath;
    
    // Iterating through all possible flight paths and calculating the cost of each path
    for (int i = startCity; i <= endCity; i++) {
        // Calculating the cost of the current path
        double currentPathCost = calculatePathCost(i, airplane, weather, airTraffic);
        
        // Checking if the current path cost is lower than the optimal path cost
        if (currentPathCost < optimalPathCost) {
            // Updating the optimal flight path vector
            optimalFlightPath.clear();
            optimalFlightPath.push_back(i);
            // Updating the optimal path cost
            optimalPathCost = currentPathCost;
        }
    }
    
    // Returning the optimal flight path vector
    return optimalFlightPath;
}

// Defining a function to calculate the fuel consumption
double calculateFuelConsumption(int startCity, int endCity, airplaneState &airplane, weatherConditions &weather, airTraffic &airTraffic) {
    // Initializing the fuel consumption
    double fuelConsumption = 0.0;
    
    // Iterating through all cities in the flight path
    for (int i = startCity; i <= endCity; i++) {
        // Calculating the fuel consumption for the current city
        fuelConsumption += calculateCityFuelConsumption(i, airplane, weather, airTraffic);
    }
    
    // Returning the total fuel consumption
    return fuelConsumption;
}

// Defining the dynamic programming algorithm
double optimizeFlightPath(int startCity, int endCity, airplaneState &airplane, weatherConditions &weather, airTraffic &airTraffic) {
    // Initializing the optimal cost
    double optimalCost = DBL_MAX;
    
    // Iterating through all cities in the flight path
    for (int i = startCity; i <= endCity; i++) {
        // Calculating the cost of the current path
        double currentPathCost = calculatePathCost(i, airplane, weather, airTraffic);
        
        // Calculating the cost of the remaining path
        double remainingPathCost = optimizeFlightPath(i+1, endCity, airplane, weather, airTraffic);
        
        // Calculating the total cost of the current path
        double totalPathCost = currentPathCost + remainingPathCost;
        
        // Checking if the total cost of the current path is lower than the optimal cost
        if (totalPathCost < optimalCost) {
            // Updating the optimal cost
            optimalCost = totalPathCost;
        }
    }
    
    // Returning the optimal cost
    return optimalCost;
}

29/04/23, 17:14 - Himral: int TSP_DP(int cost_m[][N],int n,int mark,int position)
{
  if(mark==completed_visit)
  { 
     return cost_m[position][0];
  }
  if(TSP_dp[mark][position]!=-1)
  {
     return TSP_dp[mark][position];
  }
  int res = MAX;
  for(int city=0;city<N;city++)
  {
    if((mark&(1<<city))==0)
    {
      int newAnswer = cost_m[position][city] + TSP_DP(cost_m,n,mark|(1<<city),city);
      res = min(res, newAnswer);
    }
  }
  TSP_dp[mark][position] = res;
  return TSP_dp[mark][position];
}

01/05/23, 23:39 - Himral: #include<iostream>
#include<vector>
#include<stack>
#include<queue>
#include<map>
#include <chrono>
#define N 4
#define MAX 9999
using namespace std;
using namespace std::chrono;
int dp[1000][1000];
vector<int> final_path(N + 1);
int final_res = INT_MAX;
bool isSubsetSum(vector<int> factories, int n, int sum)
{
    if (sum == 0)
        return true;
    if (n == 0)
        return false;
    if (factories[n - 1] > sum)
        return isSubsetSum(factories, n - 1, sum);
    return isSubsetSum(factories, n - 1, sum) || isSubsetSum(factories, n - 1, sum - factories[n - 1]);
}
int count_subsets_recursive(vector<int> factories, int n, int sum)
{
    if (sum == 0)
        return 1;
    else if (sum != 0 && n == 0)
        return 0;
    else if (factories[n - 1] > sum)
        return count_subsets_recursive(factories, n - 1, sum);
    else
        return count_subsets_recursive(factories, n - 1, sum) + count_subsets_recursive(factories, n - 1, sum - factories[n - 1]);
}
int count_subsets_DP(vector<int> factories, int n, int sum)
{
    if (sum == 0)
        return dp[n][sum] = 1;
    else if (sum != 0 and n == 0)
        return dp[n][sum] = 0;
    if (dp[n][sum] != -1)
        return dp[n][sum];
    else if (factories[n - 1] > sum)
        return dp[n][sum] = count_subsets_DP(factories, n - 1, sum);
    else
        return dp[n][sum] = count_subsets_DP(factories, n - 1, sum) + count_subsets_DP(factories, n - 1, sum - factories[n - 1]);
}
static int m = 0;
void printAllfactoryGroups_recursion(vector<int> factories, int n, vector<int> v, int sum)
{
    if (sum == 0)
    {
        cout << "Group of factories - " << m + 1 << ": ";
        m++;
        for (int x = 0; x < v.size(); x++)
        {
            cout << "{" << v[x] << "}"
                 << " ";
        }
        cout << endl;
        return;
    }
    if (n == 0)
    {
        return;
    }
    printAllfactoryGroups_recursion(factories, n - 1, v, sum);
    v.push_back(factories[n - 1]);
    printAllfactoryGroups_recursion(factories, n - 1, v, sum - factories[n - 1]);
}
void printAllSubsets(vector<int> factories, int n, int sum)
{
    vector<int> v;
    cout << "All possible groups of factories required to avoid wastage of closet [RECURSIVE APPROACH]:\n";
    printAllfactoryGroups_recursion(factories, n, v, sum);
}
class SubSet
{
public:
    stack<int> solutionSet;
    bool hasSolution;
    int m = 0;
    void solve(vector<int> &factories, int s, int idx, int sum, int n)
    {
        if (s > sum)
        {
            return;
        }
        if (s == sum)
        {
            hasSolution = true;
            displaySolutionSet();
            return;
        }
        for (int i = idx; i < n; i++)
        {
            solutionSet.push(factories[i]);
            solve(factories, s + factories[i], i + 1, sum, n);
            solutionSet.pop();
        }
    }
    void displaySolutionSet()
    {
        stack<int> temp;
        cout << "Group of factories - " << m + 1 << ": ";
        m++;
        while (!solutionSet.empty())
        {
            cout << "{" << solutionSet.top() << "}";
            temp.push(solutionSet.top());
            solutionSet.pop();
        }
        cout << '\n';
        while (!temp.empty())
        {
            solutionSet.push(temp.top());
            temp.pop();
        }
    }
};
void find_Min_cost_Route_GREEDY(int tsp[][N],int n)
{
	int sum = 0;
	int counter = 0;
	int j = 0, i = 0;
	int min = INT_MAX;
	map<int, int> visitedRouteList;
	visitedRouteList[0] = 1;
	int route[N];
	while (i < N && j < N)
	{
		if (counter >= N - 1)
		{
			break;
		}
		if (j != i && (visitedRouteList[j] == 0))
		{
			if (tsp[i][j] < min)
			{
				min = tsp[i][j];
				route[counter] = j + 1;
			}
		}
		j++;
		if (j == N)
		{
			sum += min;
			min = INT_MAX;
			visitedRouteList[route[counter] - 1] = 1;
			j = 0;
			i = route[counter] - 1;
			counter++;
		}
	}
	i = route[counter - 1] - 1;

	for (j = 0; j < N; j++)
	{

		if ((i != j) && tsp[i][j] < min)
		{
			min = tsp[i][j];
			route[counter] = j + 1;
		}
	}
	sum += min;
	cout<<(sum);
}
class TSP_Branch_Bound
{
public:
    bool visited[N];
    void copyToFinal(int curr_path[])
    {
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
            final_path[i] = curr_path[i];
        final_path[N] = curr_path[0];
    }
    int firstMin(int **cost_matrix, int i)
    {
        int min = INT_MAX;
        for (int k = 0; k < N; k++)
            if (cost_matrix[i][k] < min && i != k)
                min = cost_matrix[i][k];
        return min;
    }
    int secondMin(int **cost_matrix, int i)
    {
        int first = INT_MAX, second = INT_MAX;
        for (int j = 0; j < N; j++)
        {
            if (i == j)
                continue;

            if (cost_matrix[i][j] <= first)
            {
                second = first;
                first = cost_matrix[i][j];
            }
            else if (cost_matrix[i][j] <= second &&
                     cost_matrix[i][j] != first)
                second = cost_matrix[i][j];
        }
        return second;
    }
    void TSPRec(int **cost_matrix, int curr_bound, int curr_weight,
                int level, int curr_path[])
    {
        if (level == N)
        {
            if (cost_matrix[curr_path[level - 1]][curr_path[0]] != 0)
            {
                int curr_res = curr_weight +
                               cost_matrix[curr_path[level - 1]][curr_path[0]];
                if (curr_res < final_res)
                {
                    copyToFinal(curr_path);
                    final_res = curr_res;
                }
            }
            return;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
        {
            if (cost_matrix[curr_path[level - 1]][i] != 0 &&
                visited[i] == false)
            {
                int temp = curr_bound;
                curr_weight += cost_matrix[curr_path[level - 1]][i];

                if (level == 1)
                    curr_bound -= ((firstMin(cost_matrix, curr_path[level - 1]) +
                                    firstMin(cost_matrix, i)) /
                                   2);
                else
                    curr_bound -= ((secondMin(cost_matrix, curr_path[level - 1]) +
                                    firstMin(cost_matrix, i)) /
                                   2);

                if (curr_bound + curr_weight < final_res)
                {
                    curr_path[level] = i;
                    visited[i] = true;
                    TSPRec(cost_matrix, curr_bound, curr_weight, level + 1,
                           curr_path);
                }

                curr_weight -= cost_matrix[curr_path[level - 1]][i];
                curr_bound = temp;
                for (int i = 0; i < sizeof(visited); i++)
                {
                    visited[i] = false;
                }
                for (int j = 0; j <= level - 1; j++)
                {
                    visited[curr_path[j]] = true;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    void TSP(int **cost_matrix)
    {
        int curr_path[N + 1];
        int curr_bound = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < N + 1; i++)
        {
            curr_path[i] = -1;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < N + 1; i++)
        {
            visited[i] = 0;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
            curr_bound += (firstMin(cost_matrix, i) +
                           secondMin(cost_matrix, i));

        curr_bound = (curr_bound & 1) ? curr_bound / 2 + 1 : curr_bound / 2;

        visited[0] = true;
        curr_path[0] = 0;
        TSPRec(cost_matrix, curr_bound, 0, 1, curr_path);
    }
};

int completed_visit = (1 << N) - 1;
int TSP_dp[16][4];

int TSP_DP(int cost_m[][N],int n,int mark,int position)
{
  if(mark==completed_visit)
  { 
     return cost_m[position][0];
  }
  if(TSP_dp[mark][position]!=-1)
  {
     return TSP_dp[mark][position];
  }
  int res = MAX;
  for(int city=0;city<N;city++)
  {
    if((mark&(1<<city))==0)
    {
      int newAnswer = cost_m[position][city] + TSP_DP(cost_m,n,mark|(1<<city),city);
      res = min(res, newAnswer);
    }
  }
  TSP_dp[mark][position] = res;
  return TSP_dp[mark][position];
}

16/09/23, 17:20 - Himral: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

void swapIfGreater(long long arr1[], long long arr2[], int ind1, int ind2) {
    if (arr1[ind1] > arr2[ind2]) {
        swap(arr1[ind1], arr2[ind2]);
    }
}

void merge(long long arr1[], long long arr2[], int n, int m) {
    // len of the imaginary single array:
    int len = n + m;

    // Initial gap:
    int gap = (len / 2) + (len % 2);

    while (gap > 0) {
        // Place 2 pointers:
        int left = 0;
        int right = left + gap;
        while (right < len) {
            // case 1: left in arr1[]
            //and right in arr2[]:
            if (left < n && right >= n) {
                swapIfGreater(arr1, arr2, left, right - n);
            }
            // case 2: both pointers in arr2[]:
            else if (left >= n) {
                swapIfGreater(arr2, arr2, left - n, right - n);
            }
            // case 3: both pointers in arr1[]:
            else {
                swapIfGreater(arr1, arr1, left, right);
            }
            left++, right++;
        }
        // break if iteration gap=1 is completed:
        if (gap == 1) break;

        // Otherwise, calculate new gap:
        gap = (gap / 2) + (gap % 2);
    }
}

int main()
{
    long long arr1[] = {1, 4, 8, 10};
    long long arr2[] = {2, 3, 9};
    int n = 4, m = 3;
    merge(arr1, arr2, n, m);
    cout << "The merged arrays are: " << "\n";
    cout << "arr1[] = ";
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cout << arr1[i] << " ";
    }
    cout << "\narr2[] = ";
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        cout << arr2[i] << " ";
    }
    cout << endl;
    return 0;
}
